Receiving Important Domestic News 62

Military police and gendarmerie in the Hebei area are densely deployed like pieces on a chessboard, shuttling back and forth as if in broad daylight. Those with suspicious behavior are also searched. The lighting is very bright at night. After 9:00 PM every night, pedestrians are cut off. The gates of various agencies are heavily guarded and new gate passes are changed. A bomb was found on Dongmalu Bian Road the night before. The bomb was covered in a watermelon rind. Judging from its intention, if someone kicked the watermelon rind, it would explode. Fortunately, no one kicked it, otherwise, it would be in a busy area and I don't know how many people would be killed or injured. Since yesterday, inspections of ships entering and leaving the port have begun. The intersections of various concessions have also been guarded by police and gendarmerie. Pedestrians are inspected when they travel back and forth at night. Also, due to the discovery of bombs on Dongmalu, the Henan area has also been under special martial law since today. Cinemas close early at 10:00 PM. Various theaters and miscellaneous markets also stop performing at 11:00 PM. However, due to martial law, there are few patrons, and it is feared that they will all stop performing soon. Residents in the Hebei area have now begun to move to the concessions. Rents in the concessions were reduced by less than half a year, and now they are increasing again in response to the times. (August 31st)

Rampant Banditry in Yancheng 63

Yancheng County, Jiangsu Province, is located on the coast and has always been an important town in Jiangbei. Recently, due to the unrest in the current situation, Ma Yuren secretly colluded with the Northwest, and sneaked back to Yancheng, calling himself a military commander. He gathered thousands of bandits from his old troops, such as Liu Hanmin and Zhou Xiangting, spread throughout the cities and villages of Yancheng, rampaging without restraint. Wherever they passed, houses were turned into ruins, people were killed and set on fire, people were kidnapped for ransom, and self-defense guns were confiscated. They did all kinds of evil, especially in the northwest and southwest areas of the county, which were the most severely affected. In the villages and towns they occupied, people fled. Within dozens of miles nearby, no one could be seen. The county government and the county police team were perfunctory and irresponsible, only seeking to protect the county seat. Although there were hundreds of reports of robbery and distress from the four townships every day, they were ignored. The provincial government had previously sent the 133rd Brigade of the 45th Division to Yancheng to suppress the bandits. On the 24th of last month, they had brief contact with the bandits in the Sanguandian Dongzhengzhuang area in the west township, but the bandits dispersed immediately, and the officers and soldiers did not pursue them. Now the bandits are still entrenched in Xidang, robbing as usual, and even openly summoning township chiefs, setting a deadline for paying a certain amount of silver, otherwise they will burn and kill residents to their heart's content. Residents are forced to flee and seek refuge, and some have no home to return to. Although the autumn harvest is richer than in previous years, what has been harvested has been robbed by bandits, and what has not been harvested has been occupied by bandits. Traffic is blocked and business is not working. The suffering of the Yancheng people this time is probably unprecedented in the past hundred years.

According to a newcomer from Yancheng to the province, in July, Ma Yuren was appointed by Yan Xishan to return to Jiangbei to disturb Hexing Town at the Sheyang River Estuary. He gathered his old troops, contacted bandits, and gathered more than 2,000 people. Everything east of Fantai was almost completely burned and plundered, especially Xintan Chaogang and other places in Beiqizao, which were the most severely affected, because there were more than 300 guard guns there, which had assisted officers and soldiers in suppressing the bandits. When the soldiers left and the bandits came, they arbitrarily burned and killed. The Liu family, with more than 20 people, only three escaped. Around August 20th, Ma Yuren led his team west because there was nothing to plunder east of Fantai, entrenched around Dongzhuang, Zhengzhuang, and around the Liangxiang Township in Yancheng, collecting guns and extorting money from household to household. If they disobeyed, they would set fire. Cries were heard everywhere, and the fires raged. After being besieged by officers and soldiers, they fled west again and again. Now, Ma Yuren personally leads more than 2,000 people, entrenched in Xidang, Shajiazhuang, Gujiazhuang, Peijiatuan, Jiangying, Xi'an, Fengluo, Chaobao, Linshangzhuang, Jiangjiabao and other places, forcing wealthy households to supply bullets and money, middle-class households to provide rice, and the poor to provide labor. Their brutal behavior is also becoming increasingly fierce. People mostly hide in grass houses or rice fields, and some bandit leaders, such as Wu Jinbiao, who once served as the captain of the police team in Yancheng County, have more than 200 people and their behavior is slightly more lenient. They only want guns and money, and do not burn and kill at will. The officers and soldiers stationed in Yancheng and Fuyu, a certain regiment of the 133rd Brigade of the National Army, had fought fiercely with the bandits twice. Once (August 14th) in Xiangjiawei, Funing, the officers and soldiers attacked in seven routes and killed dozens of bandits. They took advantage of the victory to attack Hexing Town, but Ma had led his troops away earlier. Once (August 25th) in Dongzhengzhuang, Ma Yuren personally directed the bandits to resist stubbornly. After a day of fierce fighting, both sides suffered casualties. In the end, the bandits lacked bullets and were defeated and fled west. It is said that Ma's son, Yide, drowned in the water while fleeing in panic. It is a pity that the officers and soldiers failed to pursue and search thoroughly, causing them to regroup in Xidang and become rampant as before, which is a great pity.

Jiangxi Provincial Military Conference for Suppressing Bandits 64

Request He Yingqin to Expedite the Plan for a Joint Suppression

Nanchang Correspondence: Provincial Chairman Lu Dipin believes that the Special Task Force 123 sent by the Central Government has successively arrived in Xunyang, and the 50th Division of Tan Daoyuan has also arrived in Ganzhou one after another. The Zhu Regiment of Zhejiang arrived in Yushan Guangfeng at the end of last month. A regiment sent by Guangdong Province to Ganzhou for joint defense has also arrived in Ganzhou. Together with Zhang Huihuan and Deng Ying's two divisions and Ma Kun's brigade of the 12th Division originally in the province, and the two regiments of the Provincial Government's Garrison Regiment, the military strength is nearly four divisions, and it is the right time to suppress the bandits on a large scale. Lu convened a military conference in the provincial government the day before yesterday. The attendees included Jia Botao, the liaison staff of the Three-Province Bandit Suppression Headquarters sent by He Yingqin, all the members of the provincial government, Xiao Wenduo, the chief of staff of the 9th Route Army, and Xie Muhan, the director of the staff office. Lu served as the chairman. After the meeting, he reported on the recent bandit situation and the situation of suppression. Then, Lu Xiaochen, Wang Yinxi and others reported on the progress of the Three-Province Bandit Suppression Conference and all the resolutions. Many important cases were discussed, and it was decided to recommend Jia Botao to return to Hankou and report everything to Director He, requesting instructions and asking him to expedite the issuance of a concrete plan for the joint suppression of the three provinces in order to launch a large-scale suppression. Lu also visited Tan Division and Yue Sen Brigade, who had fought in Hunan, Hubei, Lu and Yu, and took a special train on the Nanshan Road to Tujiapu on the morning of the 5th to offer condolences and speak to all the officers and soldiers of the brigade, and returned to the province in the evening. In addition, Lu Xiaochen, the Director of the Security Office, in order to fundamentally eliminate the bandits, submitted a report to the provincial government on the strict implementation of the conscription system. The provincial government has already instructed to approve it. First, a few dozen people each will be conscripted from Yujiang, Leping, and Lichuan counties, which have not been ravaged by the bandits and where the people are honest and brave, and will be incorporated into the 3rd Guard Regiment for trial. (September 5th)

Jilin Province Raises Disaster Relief Funds for Liaoning 65

Jilin Correspondence: At the beginning of the month, a major flood occurred in western Liaoning. Provincial Chairman Zhang Zuoxiang, feeling the neighborly friendship and unable to sit idly by, ordered the Finance Department to remit 100,000 Jiyang yuan on the 20th of this month to the Liaoning government to help provide emergency relief. At the same time, charitable organizations will raise additional funds and send them one after another to provide assistance. However, the disaster is extremely serious, and the donations from various parties are small and difficult to reach everyone. The Liaoning government, upon the order of Commander Zhang, expanded the scope of relief and sent telegrams to various parties seeking relief to benefit the victims. The provincial government received this telegram last night and recorded it as follows: Jilin Provincial Government Honorable Sirs, and to all agencies, organizations, and newspapers: The counties in the western part of our province are located in the lower reaches of the rivers and are low-lying, and are frequently affected by floods. Recently, due to continuous rain and mountain torrents, the rivers have overflowed at the same time, and the dikes have collapsed. After our government sent personnel to investigate and according to reports from various counties, from Suizhong Jin County Yi County Beizhen Panshan Heishan Zhangwu in the west to Xinmin Liaozhong Taian, the area is 600 to 700 miles long and 200 to 300 miles wide, all flooded and turned into a swamp. More than 10,000 people have been drowned, tens of thousands of houses have been washed away, and no less than 400,000 to 500,000 refugees are trapped by water without food or clothing. When the flood suddenly came, they could not escape in time. Some climbed onto roofs and trees, calling for help from afar. Some houses collapsed, and they ended up being companions with the water spirits. Even worse, entire villages were trapped, without food for more than ten days. The road was far and the water was deep, and there was no way to provide relief. As a result, every household became hungry and the whole family died. After the water receded, the disaster victims had no home to return to. They either relied on begging to survive or relied on porridge pots to live. It is unbearable to witness such heartbreaking scenes. Situations like this are difficult to describe in detail. The land affected by the water was covered by sand and can never be cultivated again. This extraordinary disaster is unprecedented in nearly a hundred years. We have already ordered all counties to rush to provide emergency relief, and have first allocated funds from the provincial treasury to purchase grain for relief. At the same time, we have organized a Flood Disaster Emergency Relief Association to collect donations. We also hope that your province will allocate 100,000 Jiyang yuan, which has already been distributed in advance. However, the disaster area is vast and there are many refugees. This is just a drop in the bucket. Winter is approaching soon, and winter relief must be planned in advance. Thinking about the future, we are filled with anxiety. In addition to asking the Central Government and other provinces for relief, we hope that public and private parties in your province, either out of neighborly friendship or out of concern for our hometown, will generously donate and raise funds as soon as possible to benefit the victims. We urgently telegraph and respectfully hope for your consideration. Liaoning Provincial Government (Official Seal). After receiving the telegram, Chairman Zhang plans to

Convene a meeting of all parties within the next few days to discuss the method. (August 31st)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 66

County Government Meeting Minutes: The county government held its 73rd county government meeting yesterday to discuss the following matters: (1) The Public Security Bureau previously submitted a case requesting that the township and district chiefs pay for police rice and subsidies. The district chiefs' meeting resolved that the housing police donation has been increased and cannot be increased any further. The motion for reconsideration was resolved: The county government still orders the districts to seriously rectify the housing police miscellaneous donations to offset the costs. If there is a shortfall, it will be supplemented from the district's business expenses. (1) Previously, in accordance with the provincial promulgation of the Rules for District Chief's Offices, the district administrative expenses were reduced. It was decided that it will be implemented from September. According to the difficulties reported by various district members, the original budget will still be issued. How should this be handled? It was decided that the statements made by various districts are true. The county government will issue 60% of the original budget and submit it to the department for approval. Before instructions are received, the original budget will be temporarily paid. (1) The First District Office submitted a request to divert half of the funds from the fine item to subsidize the Public Security Bureau's Second Branch Office for housing repair expenses. Should this be approved? It was decided that fines for violations of police regulations have been approved for purchasing clothing. Whether the repair expenses are real, the county should inspect and send the repair bills to the Public Security Bureau for review, and then the matter will be reviewed.

Change of Post Office Director: Duan Changkang, the director of the local post office branch, has been in office for more than ten years. He has achieved considerable success in handling postal affairs. He has now been ordered by his superiors to be transferred to Jiading as the director. The vacancy will be filled by Xu Renzhi, the director of Jiading Post Office. Director Xu has come to Songjiang to take office.

Suzhou 67

Youth Distributes Reactionary Leaflets: Yesterday (7th), someone in Xiaojia Lane in the city distributed reactionary leaflets. The second sub-station in charge reported this to the Public Security Bureau, which dispatched patrol officer Wang Du of the bicycle team to inspect pedestrians in the area around Guanqian Street together with Patrol Officer You of the Second District. At 1:00 PM, a youth was found at Fangqiao, holding a bunch of Suzhou Youth League leaflets of the Chinese Communist Party. He was immediately taken to the bureau for interrogation. The youth spoke with a Jiangyin accent and was only in his twenties.

Escaping with a Weapon Arrested and Handled According to Law: Pei Shihua, a policeman from the Wuxi Public Security Bureau, escaped with a weapon, selling a Mauser pistol to Liu Desheng in Wangting for fifty yuan. Yesterday (7th), after the bureau chief Duan Qitang found out, he personally went to Wangting to arrest Pei and Liu and take them to Wuxi for investigation.

Wuxi 68

A Rascal Gang Beats a Woman to Death: At Maojingbang outside the North Gate of Xiyi, there lived a Jiangbei man named Bao Degao, who worked as a tailor. He lived with his mother, Dou Cai Shi, 43 years old. The two of them worked diligently to make a living. At the end of last month, a local rascal named Zhang Sanqi extorted money from Degao. Degao immediately asked his cousin, Pu Minghong, to step forward to reason with Zhang. As a result of the negotiation, Degao agreed to pay Zhang twenty yuan, first paying twelve yuan, and then wrote an IOU for the remaining eight yuan, stating that the monthly interest rate was seven percent. On the fifth of this month, Zhang Sanqi went to demand the outstanding payment. Degao had already fled to avoid him, so Zhang demanded payment from Dou Cai Shi. Cai Shi refused to acknowledge the debt, saying that her son had been frightened away and was nowhere to be found. Zhang left in anger, and soon after led five or six of his gang to the Bao home. They grabbed Cai Shi and beat her severely, causing her to fall to the ground injured. The rascals then scattered. After being beaten, Cai Shi's injuries worsened day by day, and she eventually died yesterday. The Tutheng of Tian Si Tu reported the matter to the county for an autopsy. The autopsy revealed minor injuries sustained before death, and that she had died of illness. After the autopsy, Pu Minghong, the deceased's cousin, was instructed to prepare for the coffin and burial. Meanwhile, the county government dispatched police to strictly arrest the murderers and bring them to justice.

Petition to Revoke Tobacco Bond Denied: The Second Special Tax Bureau stationed in Xiyi previously received instructions from the Translation Bureau, ordering it to collect two percent of Tobacco Warehouse Bonds along with the seven taxes on cotton, coal, paper, silk, woven goods, bamboo, and wood, with a deadline for remittance to the province. After receiving the order, Director Wang Shou Peng immediately complied. Recently, the County Chamber of Commerce reported that various businesses considered the collection of bonds along with taxes by the Special Bureau to be akin to coercion and requested the province to revoke the order, citing past precedent. After receiving the report, the bureau immediately submitted petitions to the Ministry of Finance and the Special Commissioner of Finance for Jiangsu Province, requesting revocation to appease the public and avoid criticism. The County Chamber of Commerce received an order from the Ministry of Finance, stating that the collection of two percent of rolled tobacco bonds was decided by the Executive Yuan and must be complied with. The request for revocation was denied because the matter concerned a unified plan. After receiving the order, the Chamber immediately forwarded it to various relevant industries for notification. Furthermore, at the end of last month, the Wuxi General Tax Office also received instructions from the Department of Finance, ordering it to solicit one million yuan in customs bonds. After receiving the order, Director Wang Xinru immediately convened a meeting of all branch directors in the county to discuss the matter. It was decided to first advance one-quarter of the amount, totaling two thousand five hundred yuan, to the province for urgent use. Meanwhile, the various branches solicited contributions from passing boatmen, regardless of the amount, ranging from a few cents to several yuan, and issued temporary receipts issued by the Special Commissioner of Finance, which would be exchanged for formal customs bonds in the future, with a monthly interest rate of eight percent and repayment in installments.

Collapse Injures Many in Nanyan Market: In Hongsheng Li, Eleventh District (Nanyan Market), there were four flat houses along the river, built by a local resident. Two of the houses were rented to Hua Wenqing to open a small teahouse, and the other two were rented to Chen Jingen to set up a fresh fish stall. Both businesses were doing well. However, at nine o'clock on the morning of the previous day, the houses suddenly collapsed completely due to years of disrepair. At that time, there were dozens of villagers sipping tea in the teahouse. Suddenly, they heard a loud noise and knew something was wrong. Most of them hid under the tables, so they only suffered minor injuries. However, elderly people and children were unable to escape and were injured by the collapse. Among them, Zhou Qifeng and his wife (both over sixty years old) from Nanqian Township were the most seriously injured and their lives were in danger. Chen Jingen's wife (25 years old), who was seven months pregnant, was also trapped and seriously injured. Her husband, Jingen, took her to the hospital for treatment by boat.

Apprentice Who Was Fascinated by Swordsmen Returns to Wuxi: Jia Shixing, Fan Futang, and Lv Duansheng, apprentices at the Xinji Rice Shop outside the North Gate of the town in Sanliqiao, usually enjoyed reading martial arts novels and admired swordsmen. They secretly agreed to leave on the pretext of visiting teachers on the twenty-sixth of last month. Later, the families found the three in Beijing. Only one of them, Lv Duansheng, was determined to join the army and could not be brought back. His father, Lv Jinkui, was extremely anxious and recently asked his friend to speak to Chen, the company commander of the Seventh Infantry Company affiliated with the teacher, requesting that he be allowed to return. Chen agreed, and he was escorted back to Wuxi by a friend on the morning of yesterday (the 7th).

Changzhou 69

Police Detectives Seek to Arrest Gang Leader, Fail: The Shanghai Public Security Bureau recently apprehended bandits involved in a kidnapping case, who confessed that the leader was Tang Lao Er, and that his base was in Lijiatang, Hengshanqiao, Changzhou. The bureau dispatched Captain Qi Haitian of the Arrest Team, along with detectives and a kidnap victim as an informant, to Changzhou on the 4th. They submitted a document to the county government, and County Magistrate Wu immediately sent Police Squad Leader Zhao Yongfu and his police to assist in the arrest. They arrived at the kidnappers' base in Lijiatang and found newly built, very solid houses. Inside, they found cartridge cases, bullets, photographs, and other items. Tang's wife was at home, but Tang and his concubine had gone to Taiping Temple in Lulu to offer prayers. The police detectives immediately rushed to Taiping Temple, but the bandit had received a message from his accomplices and had already fled by boat to Taihu Lake. Only Tang's mother-in-law, Wang Chen Shi, was left at the temple. The police detectives suspected that the monk Daoming was harboring bandits and took Wang Chen Shi and Daoming into custody on the 6th and sent them to the county after a preliminary hearing.

Customs Bonds, Initial Remittance of 35,000 Yuan: The Wuyi County Government Finance Bureau was ordered to raise 160,000 yuan in customs bonds, to be remitted to the provincial government in three installments, and to use this year's grain tax remittance as collateral. County Magistrate Wu and Director Liu consulted with the financial community and borrowed 35,000 yuan at a monthly interest rate of 1.3%, in accordance with the provincial order that the first installment be remitted before September 5th.

Changshu 70

Robbery and Murder Occur in Luhe Town: More than ten bandits armed with pistols arrived in Luhe Town, on the border of Changshu and Taicang, the night before last. They first broke into the Cui family's hotel, robbing all the silver jewelry and abducting five people, including Cui Zhongzhi and his family relatives. They then went to the Ma family's sundries store to rob items and abduct an employee. In the Cao family's Beijing goods store, in addition to searching for property, they also abducted an employee. After the robbery, the bandits abducted the hostages. However, Cui Zhongzhi was old and had difficulty walking, so several bandits had to help him along. When they passed the Zhou Ming Bridge in Changshu (five miles from Luhe), the bandits saw that the tofu shop owned by Chen Xing was open and dragged Chen Xing inside to help them carry the hostages. When they reached the Jiepai River, they had each of the hostages board a boat and escape towards the Yangtze River. At that time, they also planned to abduct Chen Xing, but Chen resisted. The bandits then stabbed Chen Xing in the top of the head, throat, and temples four times with a knife and threw him into the river. The district office reported the matter to the county for an autopsy. Because of the hot weather and the decaying state of the body, the family requested an exemption from the autopsy. Chen Xing's elderly mother, aged 83, depended on Chen for a living, and his wife and children are all currently in a state of mental disarray. The whereabouts of the abducted hostages are still unknown.

Public Security Bureau Organizes Big Sword Team: Recently, the Public Security Bureau of the town saw that banditry in the countryside was not peaceful. A section chief proposed to organize a Big Sword Team. The director of the Bureau and others approved the plan. It is now planned to recruit fifty team members first, and appoint Zhang Xiqing, a member of the detective team, as the instructor. Zhang is from Gushan in the town, is skilled in martial arts, and has been a boxing instructor for a long time. The preparations are currently underway.

Jiangyin 71

Acting Branch Director Shot Dead: Li Xiumin, Director of the Fifth Public Security Branch in Shengang, requested to resign from the General Bureau because his father was critically ill. After receiving a telegram from his hometown of Baoqing, Hunan, Director Li appointed Wen Cai (a graduate of the police academy from Zhouzhuang Township, Jiangyin), a probationer at the Wujin Public Security Bureau, to take his place. On the first day of his appointment, on the 6th, he went to Sigou to maintain order while Commissioner Yang of the County Government conducted an autopsy on the body of Hua Shengui, a fisherman who had been shot and killed by bandits. He returned to the Bureau at 3:00 p.m. when he was suddenly shot and killed. It is said that he was cleaning his pistol on the bed when a bullet accidentally discharged, hitting him in the chest and killing him. Director Li, upon hearing the report, personally went to the countryside to investigate that day.

Shendian Village Burned and Robbed: The home of Shen Lao Wu in Shendian Village, Zhouzhuang, Eighth District, who owned some farmland, was broken into by bandits the night before last, who set fire to the house and looted it. Eight houses were burned, and all household items were lost. Soft goods and other items were looted, for a total loss of more than four thousand yuan. The village security team went to the scene after hearing the alarm, but the bandits had already fled far away.

Zhenjiang 72

Land Registration Extended for Another Three Months: The Department of Finance, recognizing that the deadline for land registration in various counties was approaching, specifically instructed the county magistrates and directors of the Finance Bureau in all counties (except Jiangning and Zhenjiang) to extend the deadline for another three months to continue processing.

Urgent Request for Completion of Land Tax Reform Statistical Tables: The Department of Finance, regarding the reform of land tax collection and the major county finance plan in this province, previously issued statistical tables and ordered all counties to fill them out according to the format. Currently, many have not complied. Special orders were issued yesterday urging completion to facilitate review.

Punishment of Water Police Captain for Smuggling Opium: He Zhan'ao, Captain of the Twentieth Brigade of the Fifth Water Police District stationed in Jiangyin, was recently caught smuggling opium in Jiangyin by patrol boats of the Fortress Headquarters and the County Police Force. The police boat and the smuggling boat were transferred to the county government for interrogation and then reported to the provincial government for action. Director Hu, upon receiving the report, immediately ordered Jiang Chaoxiong, the District Chief of the Fifth District, to dismiss He and punish him. District Chief Jiang obeyed the order and immediately summoned the captain to the province to be placed under supervision. A successor has been appointed, Shen Hualong, to take over the post. The Department of Civil Affairs attaches great importance to this case and has dispatched a special commissioner to Cheng (Jiangyin) yesterday to investigate all the facts in detail for further investigation.

Yangzhou 73

Large Band of Bandits Attempts Robbery, Fails: In Xiannvmiao, the county, at eleven o'clock last night (the 4th)

more than a hundred armed bandits suddenly arrived, intending to first rob the guns of the Commercial Corps Public Security Bureau, and then loot extensively. When they arrived at the entrance of the commercial corps,

Page 10

they fired several shots in advance, piercing the main gate. The corps members were all asleep. Upon hearing the gunshots, they immediately got up, armed with live ammunition, and went out through the back door, engaging the bandits. Both sides exchanged dozens of shots. The aquatic public security police arrived upon hearing the alarm and surrounded the bandits. The bandits, realizing the situation was unfavorable, fled to the southwest. The commercial corps did not pursue them due to the darkness of the night. No one was injured on either side in this battle. Although the town was shocked, fortunately there was no loss.

Impersonating Inspectors, Extorting Money, Apprehended: There is a Fuyi Shun incense shop outside the West Gate of this city. The other day, a man surnamed Sun, impersonating an inspector from the military police inspection office, went to the shop and claimed to be searching for prohibited items. The shop owner asked to see his official documents, and Sun immediately brought out a certain patrol leader to vouch for him. He then extorted several hundred yuan and left. A certain inspector from the inspection office found out, went and apprehended Sun and took him to the office for punishment.

Recovered Wounded Soldiers to Depart for the Capital: All 1,400 wounded and sick soldiers in the Twenty-Seventh Rear Hospital stationed in Yangzhou were checked off and inspected one by one by personnel sent by the Ministry of Military Affairs a few days ago. It is reported that more than 800 have recovered and will be discharged from the hospital within the next few days to go to the capital and return to their respective units. It is also heard that the hospital has specially drafted twenty farewell slogans and sent them to the county party headquarters for review.

Ordering Huainan Merchants to Subscribe to 300,000 in Rolled Cigarette Bonds: The Transportation Envoy received instructions from the Ministry of Finance, ordering Huainan merchants to subscribe to 300,000 in rolled cigarette bonds. He immediately invited the merchants to a meeting to solicit contributions. The merchants, feeling that the subscriptions were too large and they were unable to comply, were mostly hesitant to proceed. Chief Ding repeatedly invited them, but only two or three people came to the office to request exemptions and asked the transportation envoy to forward their difficulties. The Ministry of Finance did not approve and ordered the transportation envoy to strictly urge them to submit the payments. The merchants reluctantly complied, and in addition to the 70,000 yuan already paid, they also sent friends to Shanghai to discuss loan methods with various banks.

Market Price of Newly Harvested Rice: Newly harvested rice has gradually entered the market in this town. Top quality is 12.8 yuan, top medium 11 yuan, standard quality 10.2 yuan, lower medium 9.3 yuan, new tail rice 8.7 yuan. It is also learned that clean, aged high-quality rice is around 15 yuan. However, unscrupulous merchants, citing continuous cloudy and rainy days, falsely claim that supplies are not abundant and have suddenly increased the price by two yuan per stone (unit of measure).

Many Deaths from Dysentery: Since the beginning of autumn, the weather has been inconsistent, and the people have been affected by the unhealthy air, causing diseases to proliferate. In recent days, many people have died from dysentery in Yangzhou City.

Nantong 74

Aftermath of Banditry in Huainan Salt Reclamation: The Dagang, Huacheng, Hede, Ougeng, and Dashen Cooperative Reclamation Companies south of Sheyang River in Huainan were occupied by bandits. The firearms of the police stationed at each company were all robbed, and the staff and tenants fled completely. On the 6th, representatives of each company held a post-disaster meeting in Nantong to discuss relief measures. Representatives who went to the province to petition reported that the province did not have enough troops to allocate to the reclamation area. It was resolved by public vote that each company would jointly organize a security corps, and 40,000 yuan was immediately raised to be submitted to the province for approval to start operations. At the same time, efforts were made to comfort the refugees, harvest flowers, and cut grass, with the aim of restoring the original situation in the shortest possible time.

Headquarters Sends Personnel to Reward Wounded Soldiers: Deng Ganping, Dai Mingxin, and Xu Guangyi were sent by the General Headquarters to Nantong, bringing funds to reward wounded soldiers. Officers received nine yuan each, and soldiers received three yuan each.

Relief for County Financial Deficit: The banditry in Tongyi has severely impacted county surtaxes, resulting in a deficit of more than 100,000 yuan. Currently, the County Finance Office is issuing 50,000 yuan in short-term public bonds with a term of six months to provide relief. All agencies must temporarily reduce their payments and will receive the balance when funds become available.

Jiaxing 75

Large Gang of Bandits Loot Two Towns: At 4:15 a.m. on the 7th, 51 bandit boats suddenly arrived at Tianningzhuang Town, located on the border between Jiaxing's northern countryside and Jiashan, and more than 400 bandits landed and looted extensively. All businesses and homes in the town were spared. The water police stationed in the town had been ordered to transfer to another location a few days ago, so when the bandits arrived, it was as if they had entered an empty land. The looting continued until after 10:00 a.m. The bandits then kidnapped Zhou Xuechi and Wang Houzai, owners of kiln households, and Zhou Zipei, owner of the Qinghao clothing store, and headed towards Taozhuang in the northern countryside. When Tianningzhuang Town was being looted, at 6:10 a.m. on the 7th, five more bandit boats arrived at Youchegang Town, about three miles away in Jiaxing County. After the bandits landed, they cut the telephone line connecting Jiaxing, and shot and killed a local security team member. Team leader Dai Hongsheng and Patrol Leader, from the police substation in the town, were arrested and taken aboard the boat, losing their freedom. The bandits then went to the Yuchang, Xinhe, Yufeng rice shops, and Yonglong Sauce Garden, and Dingyuan Pickled Fish Shop to rob (it is estimated that about 1,000 yuan was robbed from Yuchang, several hundred yuan from Xinhe and the residence, several hundred yuan from Yufeng, and about 500 yuan from Yonglong and Dingfeng). At about 8:00 a.m., the bandits released Team Leader Dai and others to the shore and sailed towards Tianningzhuang. In this incident, about 50,000 yuan was robbed from Tianningzhuang and about 4,000 yuan was robbed from Youchegang. After receiving the news, the Jiaxing Bandit Suppression Headquarters and the Water Police District Headquarters dispatched troops to give chase from the Zhiguo warship. At noon, they encountered the bandits near Taozhuang and began fighting. As of press time, the fighting was still intense.

Jiashan 76

Bandit Boats Spotted in Taozhuang, Dingzha, and Yuhui: The A'shu gang of bandits, have been pursued and suppressed by the Jiahu Bandit Suppression Headquarters, water and land military police in Qitang Baihu and Gaoxu. For the past week, things have been relatively peaceful. Now, they have mixed with the gangs from Haizhou and Henan, creating a significant force. They planned to loot near Xincang, Pinghu, but Jiaxing sent teams to suppress them. On the 5th and 6th, the bandits fled to Xiamudang in Taozhuang, with sixty or seventy boats, more than twenty boats near Dingzha, and more than ten boats in the Nanyedang of Yuhui, hoping to invade a large town in this county. Taozhuang telegraphed the county and Xitang to take appropriate precautions and reported to the Jiahu Bandit Suppression Headquarters to quickly suppress them. The towns in the northern countryside of the county are in a very critical situation. It is also reported that two or three dozen bandit boats have been spotted in Jinze and Luhu in Jiangsu, claiming that they plan to loot Xitang.

Ningbo 77

News of Replacement of Police Chiefs and Officers in the City: Police chiefs and officers under the Ningbo Public Security Bureau have been replaced by graduates of the police academy, as approved by the Department of Civil Affairs. After the official announcement, Yang Chaoqun, chief of the Second District of Jiangbei, assumed office the day before yesterday. It is now learned that Xu Yu Kuan, the officer of the First Sub-district, and Lu Nian Yang, the officer of the Second Sub-district will assume office today. Du Kui, the officer of the Third Sub-district, will take office on the 7th. Ye Zuo Ping, the officer of the First Sub-district, and Shen Zhi Ming, the officer of the Second Sub-district, have not yet arrived in Ningbo. Although Lou Wen Chao, the officer of the First Sub-district of the Third District, and Jin Ru Song, the officer of the Second Sub-district, have arrived in Ningbo, the date of their assumption is still undetermined. Liu Han Dong, the newly appointed chief of the First District of the city, arrived in Ningbo the day before yesterday. Since Director Mao thought that the chief of the First District had always been concurrently held by the director, he telegraphed the Department of Civil Affairs for instructions. After receiving the telegram, Liu was reassigned to be the chief of the Third District of the city. Liu went to the Third District in Jiangdong yesterday to discuss handover matters with the original Chief Wang. However, the date of officially taking office is still undetermined.

Loan Agreement of 250,000: Due to urgent need for funds, the provincial government planned to borrow 250,000 yuan from the local banking and money industries, and specially sent Zhu Luzhong, director of the Wuxing Unified Donation Bureau, to Ningbo to negotiate. It is learned that Director Zhu hosted a banquet for the leaders of the local banking and money industries at the Commercial Association yesterday (the 5th) at noon, with Mayor Yang, County Magistrate Chen, and standing committee members of the Commercial Association Zhang Xianlu and Yuan Weifu as guests. There were no objections during the discussion on the loan issue and agreement on the loan. However, due to concerns that the collateral would be insufficient, the provincial government was asked to find additional collateral. Director Zhu immediately agreed to go to the province to seek instructions. Regarding interest rates, since the time is short, it may be possible to follow the example of Hangzhou. It is also reported that the contract will be officially signed on the 15th of this month.

Reports of Bandit Re-Gathering in Yuyao: It is reported that Fei Zhaozhao, the bandit leader of Kan Town, Yuyao, was appointed as the commander of the Twenty-Seventh Army by Zhou Fengqi, and ordered to recruit bandits to disrupt the rear. The bandit purchased firearms, distributed them to his followers, and posted slogans to confuse people. The matter was detected by the local government, which sent troops to suppress them. The bandits fled upon hearing the news. According to reliable sources, the bandits are based in Nijiang Road, as the area is north of the coast and they can take a boat directly to Shanghai in an emergency. Moreover, it is more convenient to communicate with Zhou Fengqi, who lives in Shanghai. It is recently heard that military funds of 10,000 yuan have been remitted, and the bandits are openly placing sentries there. The number of people has reached three or four hundred. Fei's family is hiding on the sea boat, anchored in an uncertain place.

Special Dispatch

Report on the Participation of the National Private Electricity Industry Association in the World Power Conference (Continued) Li Yanshi Shen Sifang 78

(D) Dr. Atra, a Doctor of Engineering and electrical manufacturer, has extensively researched China's electrical industry and once planned to invest in the development of the electrical industry in Northeast China. Once the situation stabilizes and the government has effective measures to protect people's enterprises, it will not be difficult to realize his plan. He also advocates that the development of China's electrical industry should start with small-scale projects, which is the same as Daed Mai's view. (E) Dr. Siegel, an electrical economist, is an expert in the study of modern electrical economics and has written extensively. He advocates that commercial companies are more economical than government-run companies. The cost is lower, and due to competition among the industry, electricity prices have to be gradually reduced, unlike the extravagance of government-run companies, with large staff, disregarding economy, and often arbitrarily raising electricity prices to make up for the shortage of municipal budgets. Such things have been seen many times in European countries, and if the electrical business is run by the government, it is easily affected by politics and presents an unstable state. The government's most important obligation is to create benefits for the people to enjoy electricity, and strict management and direct control are not suitable. (F) A doctor of law and secretary of the German Employers' Association said that since Germany adopted unemployment insurance and health insurance after the war, the protection of workers can be said to be meticulous, but for every good law, there is a disadvantage that follows. Generally, bad workers often deliberately cause trouble and stop working. Once they obtain an unemployment certificate, they can sit at home and eat. The authenticity of the disease is also not necessarily a fixed standard. They often claim to be sick and do not work, and receive insurance payments to live. The current unemployment in Germany is due to sluggish foreign trade, and the disadvantages of unemployment and disease insurance are also important reasons. (7) Liaison with European academic societies. The rise of a business must have talent to take measures. China has been running schools for decades, and there are more and more people studying electrical engineering and economics management. However, the national electrical industry does not see development. Graduates from domestic and foreign specialized courses often have no opportunity to use their talents, or their studies are not used, or they are absorbed by foreign firms. This situation is most sad. Electrical enterprises cannot shirk their responsibility. The Association has learned from this and advises all colleagues to employ specialized talents as much as possible, and to communicate with students studying abroad, so that they know the current situation of domestic industries and prepare for their return home. Yan and others went to Europe this time and had considerable contact with student associations in the UK, Germany, and France, telling them that the Association humbly introduces various specialized talents, and encouraged them to serve private businesses after returning home. The results were very satisfactory. (8) Liaison with other associations. In addition to joining hands with various electrical industry associations, this trip to Europe also involved the German Oriental Association, the Engineering Society, the Electrical Engineering Society, the Employers' Association, the Standards Committee, as well as the International Electrotechnical Commission, the International Standards Committee, etc., all of which have direct or indirect relationships with the electrical industry, and have been contacted one by one to achieve the effect of mutual assistance. (9) The crisis of overdevelopment of industry in various countries. Yan and others visited industrial factories in various countries, all of which reduced work or stopped altogether due to blocked sales. The Rhine region of Germany is the center of industry, with chimneys like forests, but only half of them are lit. The number of unemployed workers is higher than in other countries. According to recent statistics, one out of every five people is unemployed. This unemployed person is indirectly supplied with life by the other four. Recently, in order to increase trade, the German government tried to reduce costs and ordered the whole country to reduce wages by 7.5%, and the products of each factory were reduced by 4% to compete with other countries. Whether it is effective is still a problem, but it can already see the danger of overdevelopment of industry. If our country does not actively develop agriculture and increase production, but only follows the lead of various industrial countries, it will only lead to death. (10) Sights on the way home. Yan and others spent two months in Europe, and various investigations and liaison work were generally in order. Because the Association's annual meeting was approaching, they had to return home early, taking the Trans-Siberian Railway, taking the opportunity to visit Soviet Russia. They departed from Berlin on the 12th of this month. The day before, Minister Jiang hosted a banquet for Qian Xing. When boarding the train, Minister Zhuang, staff of various embassies, representatives of the Power Conference, the chairman of the Oriental Association, representatives of various industrial factories, the chairman of the German Student Association, and various students all came to the station to see them off. The kindness was appreciable. After boarding the train, they arrived in Moscow on the morning of the 14th, and met with Representative Mo of the Sino-Russian Conference, and briefly inquired about the current situation in Russia, and went to the city to tour. The citizens were jostling and coming and going, all looking like beggars. The so-called national department store, with dozens of buildings, has no goods. Only a few kinds of goods are displayed in the windows, all of which are old goods, and most of them are for foreigners to buy. Domestic people are not allowed to buy without a certificate. Municipal administration is not repaired, waste is abandoned all over the ground, ashes are piled up, and the stench hits the nose. The people are hardworking and enduring, and wearing bad clothes and eating bad food, which is something that people in non-Western civilized countries can accept. From Moscow to Manchuria, for seven days and nights, what I saw along the way was that the vast plains of Siberia have been cultivated and the trees are lush. Animal husbandry is flourishing, which is very different from 20 years ago. All the large forests are harvested by the state and transported to European and Western countries for sale. Every day there are several trains, full of white pine boards and other miscellaneous trees, heading west. On the 21st, they arrived in Manchuria, on the 22nd, they arrived in Harbin, stayed in Harbin for one day, and on the 24th, they arrived in Dalian. From the Sino-Russian border to the Xing'an Mountains, there are no trees and a lack of grains for hundreds of miles. The vast area is barren land, but the soil is as fertile as Siberia. One is completely opened up and the other is abandoned. It is a pity. From Manchuria to Dalian, China takes Changchun as the boundary. The north of Changchun is the sphere of influence of Red Russia, and the south is the sphere of influence of Japan, and Japan is carrying out its colonial policy. What you can see and hear makes you wonder if you are in the three islands of Dongying. Electrical business and other public utilities have fallen into the hands of foreigners. If the people of the country do not catch up quickly, shift their eyes to the Northeast and Northwest, engage in reclamation, and work hard to build, after decades, it will not be our country. The date of the Association's second anniversary is approaching, and I am very happy to reunite with the muscle industry gentlemen and guests from all walks of life. Recalling this day last year, it was the time when the Association was born. Over the past year, it has been hard and difficult to organize internally and promote externally, and it has achieved today. The unity and consistency of the industry is gratifying, and the enthusiastic maintenance of all walks of life is especially grateful. How should we implement and improve in the future, so that the private electrical industry can develop day by day, and advance with the electrical industry of various countries in the world? Yan and others are not talented, and are willing to follow after. (End)

Important Education News

Closing Ceremony of the National Capital Party and Government Agencies' Phonetic Alphabet Training Class 79

The closing ceremony of the National Capital Party and Government Agencies' Phonetic Alphabet Training Class was held at the Zhongda Science Museum on the morning of the 6th. More than 250 people attended, including Acting Minister Liu of the Central Propaganda Department, Minister of Education, division chiefs, section chiefs, instructors, and students. At 9 o'clock, the bell rang to start the meeting. Everyone stood in silence, sang the Party song, and performed the ceremony. Chen, Acting Director of the Ministry of Education (Social Education Division), reported on the closing of the meeting. Wu Zhihui was invited to give a speech, but a reply was received stating that he could not attend. Minister Liu of the Central Propaganda Department was invited to attend the meeting for guidance and could come immediately. As for the various preparations before the meeting and the circumstances after the event, the speaker, as Acting Director, has not been in office for long. Section Chief Peng knows the details better. Please ask Section Chief Peng to report. Then Section Chief Peng Baichuan reported that the promotion of the phonetic alphabet was passed by the Second National Education Conference in April of this year, and was reviewed and approved by the 88th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Committee. The Ministry established the Ministry's Phonetic Alphabet Promotion Committee and issued 25 measures for the promotion of the phonetic alphabet in various provinces and cities, and all parties voluntarily went to do it. At the same time, various agencies sent letters hoping to organize training classes. Therefore, the training class was established. The original training period was from July 28 to September 28, two months. Later, because the Central University scheduled classes to start on September 8, the class hours were increased (the original 32 hours of separate training per group were increased to 46 hours), and the period was shortened to September 6. The training was completed. A total of 251 people from various agencies were sent to the meeting. There were 119 agencies, including 5 departments and committees under the Central Party Department, 1 municipal party department, special party departments, and 9 district party departments, 54 district branch offices, and 50 agencies in political science and law. The participants came from 19 provinces (Zhejiang, Jiangsu, Yunnan, Hunan, Guangdong, Hubei, Anhui, Fujian, Hebei, Jiangxi, Henan, Shanxi, Heilongjiang, Guizhou, Sichuan, Rehe, Shaanxi, Mongolia, Shandong) and 3 cities (Hangzhou, Peiping, Nanjing). 80% of the participants scored above 90, 16% scored above 80, and 4% scored below 80. The certificates issued this time only represent the results of the study. It is hoped that they will continue to study constantly. Then, Education Minister Jiang Menglin gave a speech. He first talked about the long history of the phonetic alphabet and the reasons why scholars did not pay attention to it and failed to promote it. Then he said that dialects are separated. If the standard sound of the phonetic alphabet is used to spell and recognize words, although it cannot unify the national language, the pronunciation will be similar and will not be too far apart and completely separated. He also talked about the usefulness of recognizing the phonetic alphabet. One is to help unify the language, and the other is to help popularize education. Everyone studied enthusiastically during the summer vacation. In the future, we will start from the capital to promote it, and popularize education, which will be a great help. He should thank everyone, etc. Then, Acting Minister Liu Yinlu of the Central Propaganda Department gave a speech, saying that Minister Jiang had spoken in detail about the usefulness of the phonetic alphabet, and he would add a little more. He thought that the Chinese nation could not be unified, not only because of the lack of military and political power, but also because of the lack of social power itself. The formation of a nation depends entirely on the natural power of society itself, and the so-called natural power is language and writing. The Netherlands and Germany, and Belgium and France, have many differences because their languages and writings are not exactly the same. Therefore, they have become independent nations. The division and merger of people depends on whether the language and writing can be unified as a measure. With natural power, then borrowing military and political power as a rescue, it is easier to unify. There are many obstacles caused by the lack of transportation and the separation of languages in the country's ethnic groups. If you want to unify language and writing, the phonetic alphabet is a simple method. Therefore, Wu Zhihui advocated it, and the Central Committee decided to promote it, in order to unify language and writing, communicate feelings and thoughts, break down the obstacles to unification, and make the nation survive firmly and have a whole spirit. Whether it is internal or external, everything can be arranged freely. I hope that everyone will be responsible for the unification work, starting from the promotion of the phonetic alphabet. Instructor Lu Yiyan summarized the main points of the speeches of Minister Jiang and Minister Liu, hoping that everyone would work hard to continue their studies, maintain what they have learned, and benefit the general public. Photo taken and meeting adjourned.

Ministry Order

Incorporating Domestic Product Production Undertakings into Teaching Materials 80

The Ministry of Education has repeatedly issued orders to promote domestic products. Now, with the approval of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, it has ordered all bookstores to incorporate domestic product production undertakings into the compilation of textbooks for geography, nature, and other subjects for primary and secondary schools, in order to promote them and cultivate them. A special order is given to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities: The Ministry of Industry and Commerce's No. 12226 document is approved. (According to the report of the Industry and Commerce Visiting Bureau of the Ministry that in order to encourage the people to purchase domestic products, it is appropriate to collect teaching materials, classify and compile them in geography, natural science and other subjects in primary and secondary school textbooks, so as to cultivate the habit of the people to love and use domestic products. Please consult the Ministry of Education for verification and handling, etc. The Ministry has carefully reviewed it and found it not without merit. The original report should be copied and consulted to your Ministry for consideration and handling.) Because of the above reasons, and a copy of the original report of the Industry and Commerce Visiting Bureau was attached to the Ministry, it was found that the Bureau's request to include the production of domestic products in primary and secondary school textbooks was not without merit. With the approval of the above reasons, in addition to replying to the consultation and issuing separate orders, the original report is hereby copied and issued to your province, ordering all bookstores in the province to incorporate the production of domestic products as much as possible when compiling textbooks for geography, nature, and other subjects for primary and secondary schools, in order to promote them and cultivate them. This is of utmost importance.

Local News

The Municipal Government Strives for the Provincial Slaughter Tax and the Jurisdiction of Shanghai Municipal Secondary Schools 82

The Shanghai Municipal Government and the Jiangsu Provincial Government are competing for the provincial and municipal slaughter tax and the Shanghai Secondary School and other schools should be placed under the jurisdiction of the city. Although the scope of authority has been divided by the administrative meeting, there are still disputes between the two sides regarding the date of transfer and takeover. Recently, the Municipal Government submitted another document to the Executive Yuan, stating that the case was submitted to the Executive Yuan for instructions. The instructions No. 2700 of the Executive Yuan stated, "Previously, the Municipal Government submitted a report stating that the Finance and Education Bureaus requested that Shanghai Secondary School and other schools be taken over immediately, or that the takeover be postponed for half a year. From January 20, the city's education tax rights and education rights should be completely handed over to the city for takeover." When the case reached the Yuan, it was sent to the Ministry of Education for consideration. Now, according to the Ministry's reply, "The case has been consulted with the Jiangsu Provincial Government for verification. Now, with the approval of the consultation reply, after investigating this case, the reasons were stated earlier and a request was made to maintain the original case, which has been approved by the Executive Yuan. Since it has not been long since then, it is not appropriate to change the decision rashly." The Ministry of Education has presented its views and is awaiting approval. After receiving this, the municipal government immediately forwarded the instructions to the Finance and Education Bureaus for their information. Now, according to the Education Bureau's report, "The issue of the management of the city's slaughter tax and the issue of the jurisdiction of Shanghai Secondary School and the Experimental Primary School were previously approved by the 60th meeting of the Executive Yuan. The measures proposed by the three ministers, Jiang, Wang, and Kong, changed the final decision due to the Jiangsu Provincial Government's one-sided request for reconsideration. The two bureaus have repeatedly submitted reports to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Education, requesting that the original decision be adhered to and that efforts be made to adhere to the original decision. It has been investigated that since the slaughter tax is revenue in the city, it should naturally belong to the city and be managed by the city. It is clearly stated in the minutes of the provincial and municipal division of governance rights that the status quo will be maintained temporarily. Negotiations have been held repeatedly over the years, but the transfer has not been made. As for Shanghai Secondary School and other schools, they are located within the city's boundaries. If they are managed by the province for a long time, the city's education administration will be divided, and the entire city's administrative region will be destroyed. The three ministers, Jiang, Kong, and Wang, have seen this and proposed to transfer them to the jurisdiction of the city and set the transfer time at the end of the 18th year. From the beginning of the takeover to the transfer time, there are four months of preparation time. However, the province said that due to the jurisdiction of educational institutions and the burden of expenses, there were many difficulties at the end of the 18th year, and it was unable to comply for a while, requesting reconsideration. The inability to comply was at the end of the 18th year, and now it is the 19th year, and the difficult time has passed. As for saying that it has not been long since then and it is not appropriate to change the decision rashly, the first time the Executive Yuan approved the measures proposed by the three ministers, Jiang, Wang, and Kong, it has not been long since then, and a request was made to reconsider and change the final decision. There is a precedent to follow, and the so-called considerable period of time is requested again for implementation. It is not clear when it can be said to be considerable. The matter concerns the city's administrative authority, and the speaker dares not to be bothered and submits another report to the superiors for verification. It is requested that the slaughter tax and other issues of Shanghai Secondary School be handled according to the original decision and returned to the jurisdiction of the city in order to clarify the functions and powers.

News from China Radio Engineering School 84

China Radio Engineering School was founded by Yu Qiaqing and other major merchants in Shanghai. The teaching and management are serious and strict, and the instruments and machinery are fully equipped. Students practice communication and reporting. A Westerner from the French radio station, Mr. Qian Shufu, is hired to guide the students at the school every day, teaching them the technology of communication and reporting on the one hand, and teaching them the principles of engineering on the other hand, so that the students can definitely undertake important work on the radio station after graduation. Graduates have been introduced by the school one after another and have obtained considerable occupations. Some have served as radio operators on major ships, and some have served as deputy engineers in various companies and radio stations. Last month, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company recruited radio operators and selected 15 people. Students from the school accounted for half of them. This autumn, the first examination for enrollment recruited more than 50 people. The second examination is scheduled for September 14. Recently, students from other provinces and cities have registered for the examination, which is unusually . The school's engineering and telecommunications departments have a quota of 100 students, and both men and women are accepted. The school is located at 855 Mengnala Road.

Results of the Women's Games at Stamford Bridge, England

Three World Records 87

One Mile Race Walk ···· 8 minutes 14 and 2/5 seconds

Half Mile Run ···· 2 minutes 18 and 1/5 seconds

Two Hundred Yard Run ···· 25 and 1/5 seconds

(London Dispatch, August 17th) The British Women's Amateur Athletic Association held a meet at Stamford Bridge on August 16th. Mrs. Howarth of the Middle-Aged Women's Sports Association, the world record holder for the one-mile race walk, had just married on August 10th. Although still enjoying the sweetness of her honeymoon, she still participated in the competition, which was also the last time in her life that she showed her skills in the one-mile race walk on the athletic field. Mrs. Howarth led in half of the one-mile race, but in the end, she was overtaken by Mrs. Mason, also of the Middle-Aged Women's Sports Association, who won the championship, defeating Mrs. Howarth by a distance of twenty-five yards. The time was recorded as 8 minutes, 14 and 2/5 seconds, which is a new world record, breaking Mrs. Howarth's previous world record of 8 minutes and 12 seconds.

Recently, at another athletic meet at Stamford Bridge, Mrs. Howarth completed a one-mile race walk in a time of 8 minutes and 12 seconds, originally a new world record. However, the track was not measured after the race, so it could not be recognized, which is a great pity. (If a result is to be recognized as a world record, the track must be re-measured immediately after the race to show caution.) Mrs. Mason's walking style was very beautiful this time, and more than three thousand spectators cheered greatly.

Another new world record was Miss Lyne's half-mile run, with a time of 2 minutes, 18 and 1/5 seconds, breaking Miss Cutlack's record of 2 minutes and 24 seconds. Miss Lyne took the lead from the start and never fell behind. Although the swift Miss Stone worked hard, she was never able to take first place. The results of each event are as follows:
