Book Introductions

Unfaithful Love 183

— Wén Zhì

By Xiàng Péiliáng

In modern Chinese literature, a very bad phenomenon can be observed: most writers are unwilling to adopt a "faithful" attitude towards our literature. They are too "unfaithful" in their creative endeavors, especially in not putting in deep effort into their area of expertise, to create a work that represents their "loyal" dedication to literature. As the saying goes, "Pork head meat is not refined in three ways." Indeed, this is very much reflected in the current literary scene. This is especially unfortunate in the field of drama. There are few authors truly dedicated to drama. Most approach dramatic creation with the attitude of "might as well give it a try." As for those who truly have ambition and constantly strive, I have yet to put a number on them.

I have carefully examined the authors dedicated to drama in the Chinese literary scene. I have also privately wished to extensively collect dramatic works since the New Culture Movement, providing detailed analyses and conducting analyses of all dramatic authors. However, due to the constraints of work, I can only do so vaguely for the time being without much confidence. However, I will not take "mirror flowers and water moon" as my expectation. However, in the past dramatic authors, I certainly have people I admire. Among them, the author of "Unfaithful Love," Xiàng Péiliáng, is one. His attitude towards drama is this: "As long as I can contribute a little to drama, like a farmer digging at least one or two hoe-fulls, even if my efforts may all be in vain, as long as I have made an effort, then I will have no regrets." Yes, when the drama movement's life in China is still very short, it needs "faithful" people like farmers to dig, even if it is only one or two hoe-fulls.

The author himself has admitted that he is going to achieve something in drama, which is indeed something I am delighted about. The author himself also believes that "the entire work of drama requires a long period of hard labor." He tells us, "From the moment an initial inspiration is grasped to the completion of the last sentence, from the intention to perform a play to the fall of the last curtain, there is endless labor involved. People without patience cannot do it." It can be seen how meticulous and hardworking he is when creating plays, fully expressing a complete life. Recently, the author's published works have mostly focused on drama. Novels are rarely seen. However, the hardship of writing plays, according to him, is that "when I was a supplement editor, I often wrote thousands of words in the morning, but none of my one-act plays took less than three months. I don't draft much when I write text and rarely revise it after completion, but plays are revised at least three times." This is truly such perseverance. These are only what I want to prove the author's rigorous attitude when writing.

"Unfaithful Love" contains two plays, "Unfaithful Love" and "Divorce." The author spent about a year writing them. These two multi-act plays are still the author's early works, because the author grasped the idea that "writing plays must start with multi-act plays." Presumably, after these two plays, it seems that the author had already switched to one-act plays. Indeed, the atmosphere of these two plays is somewhat similar to "Fleeting Dream." However, although written before "Depressing Drama," they were published not long before "Bright Drama." I think these two multi-act plays may represent the author's initial style and tendency to work and the techniques of multi-act plays, perhaps they are multi-act plays worth commemorating.

These are all based on the romance of young people, full of irony. In all of Xiang's plays, there is almost a common point, that is, the author's own vitality is very strong. Places about telling his inner feelings seem to be very clearly revealed. That vitality represents the author's own will. "Unfaithful Love" is a three-act play that tells a story in a metropolis. It begins by quoting the first and last sections of Eroshinko's lullaby as a symbol: "(The child cries, dear one cries, he cries in the cradle, although there are good toys, he does not want to be quiet and fall asleep, little child, take your toys, good children at night, are all asleep in the cradle.)" If you carefully savor these two verses, you can immediately know the suggestion that the author wants to point out to people in this tragedy. It is about a twenty-seven-year-old university graduate marrying an innocent and lovely eighteen-year-old girl whom he has known for less than half a year in a scene of unfaithful love. The male protagonist, Long Yingnan, is tired of the floating and wandering life after leaving university, without any sense of belonging. Therefore, he wants to try again one last time. His purpose is to change his inner attention with new stimulation and new pain, so he chooses marriage and love, hoping to make up for past deficiencies. They did not consider whether their personalities understood each other. "(I don't ask how he feels about my love, I'm just going to do this, take care of the present. The love I need, I will create myself.)" It can be seen that the female protagonist, Tao Yawen, has a very superficial view of "love" and has not yet formed any preconceptions.

Soon, Tao Yawen was finally bewitched by the literary writer Wu Mengyin, who specialized in writing about love, and secretly agreed to Wu Mengyin's appointment without her husband's knowledge. Although she knew that her husband's recent actions were often very reluctant and had deep, hidden sadness, she hid it and refused to express it. But she did not try to understand why her husband was so tormented. She wanted her husband not to drink, but did not dissect why her husband was thirsty for alcohol. Finally, Long Yingnan cursed after begging his wife not to go to Wu Mengyin's appointment and being rejected, "(I want to rest temporarily in love, originally wanted love as shelter, to avoid wind and rain and angry tides, the terrible invasion of civilization, but, was it a success or a failure?)" In fact, what Long Yingnan was pleasing his wife with was only for his wife's extravagance and vanity, preferring to make himself very strapped and had to borrow money from friends. He did not want to use a great career to overcome his wife, but wanted to forget the human vocation and social status. He only wanted to serve like a servant serving a master. Naturally, the woman's psychological demands would also be disappointed. However, on the one hand, Long Yingnan's pain was increasing day by day, and on the other hand, Tao Yawen's pressure also matured. In the park, Wu Mengyin used threatening means to woo Tao Yawen, even using a fake pistol to express his determination. Fortunately, Long Yingnan's friend saw through the truth and was rescued. As for this tragedy, it happened on the same day at the same location. Then, Long Yingnan also arrived. He admitted his mistake, the mistake of forcing himself to seek love "(In order to avoid the invasion of irresistible depression, I wanted to spend my whole heart and body in love, so as not to think about other things,)" and said "(I love you... this is the first time I love you, and it is also the last time I love you,)" and suddenly took out a pistol and committed suicide. Although Tao Yawen knew his heart at this time, and especially loved his willful character, it was over, because his pistol really had bullets.

Indeed, Tao Yawen's words are not without research value: "(Although he is considerate to me in every way, I never know his heart. He follows my words and caters to my meaning, but these all seem mechanical. He is reluctantly happy for me, reluctantly smiles, his words are not from the heart... I am still young, I want my own life, a reasonable life, and it is also very proper not to love such a mechanical person.)" (Page 82) This is because the buds of youth have not received true comfort, and everyone will feel bored. Therefore, young people in the times should not seek love solely based on certain demands, but rather on how to support and create this "great love."

"Divorce" is a four-act play. The story is like this: College student Zhang Jiezhi is indifferent to his wife, who, under the old etiquette and system, is said to be "only good for eating, not for showing off," and is eager for a divorce. On the one hand, he is secretly pursuing his love, hiding the fact that he is already married. His plan is to announce the divorce from his wife when love matures, but he will never tell his lover before the divorce, so as not to cause changes in the middle. Unexpectedly, when it was about to mature, a mischievous friend told his lover as much as possible, causing his lover to be furious, thinking that everything he said was a lie. His strictest fifth uncle also found out. When he was discussing the aftermath with that mischievous friend, he came to reprimand him. Therefore, the divorce plan completely failed. But who knew that all the accidents were caused by his friends betting and making trouble! Because of his friends' bets, he ruined the love he was pursuing.

Originally, young people are especially receptive to the baptism of new ideas. How can a marriage without love, arranged by the family, be satisfactory? But if the conditions for the wife are only for pleasure and happiness, "(The most important thing is to be beautiful, and the second is to be able to socialize, dance, sing, play the piano, and be interesting to take out,)" (Page 104) then it would be too ignorant and too boring to abandon one's own wife. I also believe that if things have already been done, one should also think about the future of one's own wife. In this era of transition between the old and the new, is this action harmless to her? Because the shackles of the old society have numbed her entire thinking. In the end, the only thing left is "(suicide)." Then, is it possible to remove one's personal position?

In general, these two plays are not a failure. The dialogue is very smooth, the intention is also very profound, and the structure is also tight. However, I think that compared with the one-act plays written by Xiang Jun since then, they seem to be a little worse. The expression of his one-act plays can be seen everywhere to be more powerful than multi-act plays. This is my personal opinion, what do you think, Xiang Jun?

Page 20

Wind in the Wilderness 184

— Tāng Bīn

By Mù Hóng

The "Hurricane Movement" suddenly appeared in Chinese literature, it seems to have been several years ago. Regarding this type of work, at that time, I loved to read, in addition to Peiliang's plays and novels, also Mu Hong's poems and prose, because Mu Hong's works have a new style, neither imitating Western writers, nor imitating ancient Chinese literary works, only expressing himself, such a spirit of creation, really makes us admire. In other words, this kind of literature full of true life, in China, which is called a backward culture by foreigners, needs to be produced in large quantities, but unfortunately, as far as I know, there is only Mu Hong who is still working hard recently.

Needless to say, his recent works have made even more satisfactory progress in art. I see that he does not write his works carelessly, between each sentence, it is clearly understood that he has spent a lot of energy. In terms of form, he always tends to be new. This article "Wind in the Wilderness" makes us more and more satisfied, it is really gratifyingly novel.

This article is divided into two sections, each section is divided into several subsections, full of rich poetic meaning, truly, rather than saying that he is a new form of novel, might as well say that he is a new form of lyrical poem, because the author is full of imagination, and is best at writing prose and lyrical poetry, as long as people who have read his works will believe it without any doubt.

Because what he wrote is a long poem, he naturally infused a lot of profound symbolism, in order to make a work have superhuman vitality, so that readers with slightly weaker appreciation ability cannot understand what he wrote, but can stubbornly hold on to an unusually enthusiastic heart, no matter what, to make you read it in one breath, and feel that it has a special style, this is a new masterpiece full of profound allegory, this article "Wind in the Wilderness" is of course also like this, now we can carefully look at what he wrote.

We are now desolate, desolate as water, we ourselves must pray, (Do not allow ice to freeze or disappear,) cool water can still boil and steam up,

What is this, it is obviously writing prose poems full of upward consciousness, although it is talking about the desolation of life, but then he imagined that (Cool water can still boil and steam up,) this is how humorous and profound the meaning is, so that we will not feel an unusual monotony when we read it, in these very simple words,

Our body is a lost sheep, no need to look for the old nest again, those who look for the old prison are not seen much, who said, (already cut off the waist,) today's matter, just our heads and bodies are so hard, can we exchange it for a comfortable bed to sleep a dull sleep, the lively gatherings of old friends are really courteous, we respectfully thank you for your disturbance, we still want, in the hands of peaceful people, will give a little true friendship, when not giving a bed, give a few skinny horses to run—we have been away from the battlefield for a few days, and now the flesh on our thighs is growing, itching to race a thousand miles, the moon shines on the ground, but the horse, really cute, fell off the battlefield several times, were all turned over by our jump, jumped on its waist, the enemy is in front swallowing bullets and drinking blood, we, run all the way—putting the horse in front like chasing sparrows, happy and eager, today lazy and forgot the horse, forgot, our precious baby, friends, you give us favors, when not giving a bed, give a skinny horse to run, and try the blood in the battlefield to jump, a tornado-like horse, a roll of turbulent waves is our heart, in the past crazy flying and rushing,

Heaven and earth choked their voices and did not dare to be暴躁…

This section is really written cute, in the tone is sonorous and harmonious, no less than a beautiful prose poem with rhyme, in the words, is how refined, definitely not out of the ordinary hand, carefully read down, very much like singing a great war song, prompting young people to run to the front line of the battlefield, to strive to kill the enemy, only forward can get the comfort of life, only struggle can see the light, this is the fact given to us by history, but in modern literary works, with such a forceful and beautiful writing, there are really not many, (Wind in the Wilderness)'s author, also nakedly expresses it between the lines, proclaiming it before our eyes, originally, no successful heroes and outstanding people in ancient and modern China and foreign countries, have not struggled out of ten thousand difficulties, in fact, young people in general, should never be willing to fall behind, all day long confused and dreaming of unearned dreams, now is the time of angry horses galloping, it is really not allowed for young people to continue to be so unmotivated and mixed up, at least, we read the section of prose poetry containing force and beauty quoted above, and feel that there are such thoughts,

We can even read this new form of novel by the author as a lyrical war song, because poetry is the most moving to readers, especially the rhythm is sonorous, and the emotions are heroic and passionate, great war songs are really rare in China,

The facts of the whole article are very complicated, the beginning is writing (Many hearts are entangled with a lover, but the lover is now dead,) hoping to bring a message, to know this message, of course, only from (the graveyard) or (the ghost gate) can be obtained, in fact, these many passionate hearts like fire, must strive upward, rush forward, later the protagonist in this article realized this point, and jumped on the horse, ran to the battlefield, (like the wind in the wilderness, blowing and singing to himself,) inside also mixed with many descriptions that promote people upward, finally, needless to say, it is to get a different success, as in the sixteenth section, there is already such a writing, (The revolution has succeeded,) people's hearts sing and rejoice, you go to Tibet in the west, I throw myself into the East China Sea to embrace the bright moon) which contains the meaning of unlimited life,

What we most envy is that the author divided this long lyrical poem into several sections to describe, each section has a new style, different charm, so that readers never tire of reading, so, the author wrote this article (Wind in the Wilderness) really spent a lot of thought and effort, indeed, (Mu Hong uses his popular atmosphere to write the inner petition, the mood is deep and quiet, the words are beautiful, and what is even more unique is that, in that deep quiet and beauty, he spits out a powerful and desperate breath, Wind in the Wilderness is his unique style of work), it is most appropriate to recommend Mu Hong with these words, because his works have real value, we may as well read another section of it, to make the end of this article, I think those who love his works also agree,

Life after life I can not forget your loyalty, birds flying and animals walking, how can they be the same as my drifting feelings, now I only use your body, but I follow your mood on the way,

On the way, you must walk vigorously, a living person is really useful, I love myself in the living lover, and I am willing to help him with brave blood,

My soul has been awakened by you again and again, this is like the human affection of the living, why should we be separated by hugging and kissing, I still have a living human heart, then please take this living heart back, and it is not in vain for you to indulge here for a few days, our hearts were originally the same, and will all be completed on this unfinished journey,
